       function decorate(event) {
         event = event || window.event;
         var target = event.target || event.srcElement;
         if (target && (target.getAttribute('action') || target.getAttribute('href'))) {
           ga(function (tracker) {
             var linkerParam = tracker.get('linkerParam');
             document.cookie = '_shopify_ga=' + linkerParam + '; ' + 'path=/';
           });
         }
       }
       addListener(window, 'load', function(){
         for (var i=0; i <document.forms.length; i++) {
           var action = document.forms[i].getAttribute('action');
           if(action && action.indexOf('/cart') >= 0) {
             addListener(document.forms[i], 'submit', decorate);
           }
         }
         for (var i=0; i <document.links.length; i++) {
           var href = document.links[i].getAttribute('href');
           if(href && href.indexOf('/checkout') >= 0) {
             addListener(document.links[i], 'click', decorate);
           }
         }
       });
     
 
     var originalDocumentWrite = document.write;
     document.write = customDocumentWrite;
     try { window.ShopifyAnalytics.merchantGoogleAnalytics.call(this); } catch(error) {};
     document.write = originalDocumentWrite;
 
     
         window.ShopifyAnalytics.lib.page(
           null,
           {"pageType":"home"}
         );
       
     
   });
 
   
       var eventsListenerScript = document.createElement('script');
       eventsListenerScript.async = true;
       eventsListenerScript.src = "//cdn.shopify.com/s/assets/shop_events_listener-f2c5800305098f0ebebdfa7d980c9abf56514c46d5305e97a7c476f7c9116163.js";
       document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(eventsListenerScript);
     
 })();
   </script>

           <a class="hidden-product-link" href="/products/believe-to-achieve-01725" itemprop="url">
            Believe to Achieve: See the Invisible, Do the Impossible
           </a>
           <div class="info">
            <!-- product believe-to-achieve-01725 set-price -->
            <!-- product.price 1495: wh_price 1495-->
            <!-- product.price_min 1495 : wh_price_min 1495 -->
            <!-- product.price_max 1699 : wh_price_max 1699 -->
            <!-- wh_discount_value 1 -->
            <!-- compare_at_price : wh_compare_at_price  -->

            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="books,leadership-development,new-releases-and-coming-soon-for-summer-fall-2018,paperback-books" data-compare-price="" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description="&lt;p&gt;Howard White tells us, &quot;Extraordinary people are simply ordinary people on fire with desire.&quot; Sometimes we need a hand to help unlock the gifts inside us. &lt;em&gt;Believe to Achieve&lt;/em&gt; is that helping hand, daring readers of all ages to reach for their most cherished dream and giving them the tools to get there. Full of behind-the-scenes moments with famous athletes as well as insightful anecdotes, this book is an exuberant collection of wisdom that will help readers recognize the potential in themselves and their path to success.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;In this updated and expanded 2018 edition of &lt;em&gt;Believe to Achieve&lt;/em&gt;, Howard White shows readers how to turn his hard-earned lessons into a roadmap for their own personal success. It covers such topics as positive thinking, attitude, heart, responsibility, leadership, happiness, forgiveness, truth, confidence, integrity, honor, success, balance, fear, honesty, the power of thought and mind, the inner and outer worlds, body, soul, money, friends, self, humility, sacrifice, love, and respect.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Believe to Achieve&lt;/em&gt; 2018 updated edition is a book about people. It is based on Howard's personal story, and the stories of people he has met along the way. He offers readers an insider's view from the locker room of the famous sports teams to the inner office of Nike creator and former CEO Phillip Knight. He brings readers in on conversations with some of sport's greatest icons such as Michael Jordan and Charles Barkley. At its heart however, &lt;em&gt;Believe to Achieve&lt;/em&gt; is a book about everyday heroes and the star that shines in every one us, regardless of fame or fortune. Howard believes that everyone has the power to profoundly affect the life of another by mentoring or simply caring. &quot;You never know which child holds the potential to cure cancer,&quot; he said. &quot;When you were growing up, you had people who cared about you, not necessarily your parents. Maybe the mailman or the bus driver asking you how you did in school. We have gotten away from that.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;This book offers something for everyone. Young and old alike will learn how tap the potential of the future. It is never too late to believe in yourself. People from all walks of life will find Howard's story exciting and informative. Howard illustrates the rewards of spiritual awareness, faith, and prayer in practical real-life terms that transcend the boundaries of religious dogma.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Believe to Achieve&lt;/em&gt; 2018 updated edition is a voice of encouragement that will help readers face the challenges of life with dignity and honor. It affirms that any one of us can and does make a difference. Howard believes that, &quot;It's the low points in life that that determine how high you will go.&quot; His optimism provides a heart-healing message in the face of adversity. His vision illuminates the opportunity inherent in the darkest moments. His voice calls out to the best part in all of us.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;2018 Edition, Paperback&lt;br&gt; ISBN: 978-1-58270-690-0&lt;br&gt; Pages: 224&lt;br&gt; Dimensions: 6 x 9 inches&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;2007 Edition, Paperback &lt;br&gt;ISBN: 978-1-58270-172-1 &lt;br&gt;Pages: 144 &lt;br&gt;Dimensions: 6 x 9 inches&lt;/p&gt;" data-handle="believe-to-achieve-01725" data-id="8384001928" data-images="2689777991716 || Believe to Achieve: See the Invisible, Do the Impossible ||17651034888 || Believe to Achieve: See the Invisible, Do the Impossible ||" data-initial-modal-price="" data-no-instant="" data-price="$16.99" data-regular-description='Howard White tells us, "Extraordinary people are simply ordinary people on fire with desire."             <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="dvd-blu-ray,new-releases-for-spring-2018,new-releases-and-coming-soon-for-summer-fall-2018" data-compare-price="" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description='&lt;p class="p1"&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;In 1971, forty year old Leonard Knight was picking apples on a farm in Vermont when he looked up and saw a hot air balloon advertising a beer company. He closed his eyes, had a vision, and exclaimed, “I gotta build a balloon that says, ‘Jesus’ on it!” For the next 15 years, Leonard crisscrossed the country in a multi-colored truck covered in Bible verses trying to launch a balloon he sewed together out of bedsheet-sized scrap material that read “GOD IS LOVE,” in giant tattered letters, but never got it off the ground.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p class="p1"&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;Leonard eventually ended up destitute in a remote squatter’s camp in the sweltering California desert where he decided to build a “GOD IS LOVE” mountain to proclaim his testimony. Fellow squatters coined the work, “Salvation Mountain.”&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p class="p1"&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;Humble, stubborn, artistic and outspoken, Leonard spent most of his life in isolation. Despite being orthodox in his theology, his quirky eccentricities were never appreciated by what he called “the big churches.” Reminiscent of a modern day John the Baptist, Leonard was a rock star to seekers from every walk of life and societies misfits. He had to continue on his solo path to fulfill the purpose God had planted in his heart while fending off illegitimate attacks from the county, state, and EPA. But the proud left broken, and the broken left with hope, and by 2009, thousands a week were traveling from all over the world to personally hear “the humble desert hobo” share his “love story.”&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p class="p2"&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;In his final years, already blind, deaf, and slipping into the abyss of dementia, Leonard’s ministry would face it’s greatest opposition yet, which he faced undaunted with his child-like faith. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p class="p2"&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;&lt;i&gt;The Love Story of Leonard Knight &lt;/i&gt;is an affectionate exploration of his humble beginnings, his years wandering, the moment he received his calling, and his quirky artistic project that was described in 2002 as a “National Treasure” in the US Congressional Record, and is today considered possibly the largest Biblically inspired art-installation on earth.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="dvd-blu-ray,new-releases-and-coming-soon-for-summer-fall-2018" data-compare-price="" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description="&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;This special edition DVD of &lt;em&gt;Seeing the Unseen&lt;/em&gt; includes two bonus features: &lt;em&gt;How to Build a Psychomanteum&lt;/em&gt; and &lt;em&gt;A Look at Scrying Through History&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;In Western cultures, death often means the loss of a loved one–never to speak to them again. But what if death just requires a different form of communication? For thousands of years, people all over the world have communicated with the dead using various forms of scrying, also known as clear-depth gazing. Intellectuals like John Dee, Nostradamus, Plato, and even entire civilizations such as the Aztecs, Greeks, Egyptians, Persians, and many others, used clear-depth gazing with reflective cups, pools of water, cauldrons, and mirrors so that the bereaved could continue their connection with the dead. Clear-depth gazing has been, and continues to be, a way of seeing visions of things past and moments in the future. Used by cultures primitive and advanced, scrying is seeing a resurgence in practice to “see the unseen.”&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;Enter award-winning author Dr. Raymond Moody, the leading authority on the near-death experience. After traveling to the Greek psychomanteum known as the Oracle of the Dead in Ephyra, Greece, he built his own psychomanteum to continue studying the effects of using this technique to experience contact with departed loved ones. What he discovered will forever change how we process death.&lt;/p&gt;" data-handle="seeing-the-unseen" data-id="740164861988" data-images="2705896701988 || Seeing The Unseen: The History of Using Clear-Depth Gazing for After-Death Communications ||" data-initial-modal-price="" data-no-instant="" data-price="$19.95" data-regular-description="This special edition DVD of Seeing the Unseen includes two bonus features: How to Build a Psychomanteum and A Look at Scrying Through History.             <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="books-films-and-products-exclusively-by-women,beyond-words-s-bestselling-titles,books,new,new-releases-for-spring-2018,new-releases-and-coming-soon-for-summer-fall-2018,paperback-books" data-compare-price="" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description='&lt;div class="page" title="Page 2"&gt;
 &lt;div class="layoutArea"&gt;
 &lt;div class="column"&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;How can I live authentically? What is my life’s purpose? How can I tap into my soul’s wisdom? How can I receive Divine guidance? &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;To learn the answers to these questions, gifted intuitive, visionary teacher, and author Sara Wiseman gives you &lt;/span&gt;&lt;em&gt;Messages from the Divine&lt;/em&gt;&lt;span&gt;. Timeless and affirming, the 66 lessons in this book will teach you the secrets of how to live from your soul’s wisdom, awaken to your true life’s path, and learn how to have &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;direct connection &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;with the Universe. And by living a soul-led life, you move from confusion, fear, and feeling unfulfilled to a life that is open, original, and profoundly meaningful. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;In 2000, Sara had a near death experience that resulted in a sudden opening of consciousness, allowing her natural psychic abilities to fully manifest. Her spiritual understanding expanded, and she began to see “beyond the veil” and receive messages from spirit guides. It is from this process of Divine receiving that the 66 lessons in this book were transmitted and transcribed. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Each of the 66 lessons ends with a brief exercise—an easy-to-do practice, mediation, or reflection to help anchor the teaching—along with a short collection of anecdotes from the author’s life. Lyrical in style and meditative in experience, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;em&gt;Messages from the Divine &lt;/em&gt;&lt;span&gt;will inspire, empower, and awaken your soul. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

           <a class="hidden-product-link" href="/products/the-love-story-of-leonard-knight-vod" itemprop="url">
            The Love Story of Leonard Knight VOD
           </a>
           <div class="info">
            <!-- product the-love-story-of-leonard-knight-vod set-price -->
            <!-- product.price 995: wh_price 995-->
            <!-- product.price_min 995 : wh_price_min 995 -->
            <!-- product.price_max 995 : wh_price_max 995 -->

            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="digital,new-releases-for-spring-2018,new-releases-and-coming-soon-for-summer-fall-2018,video-on-demand" data-compare-price="" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description='&lt;p class="p1"&gt;In 1971, forty year old Leonard Knight was picking apples on a farm in Vermont when he looked up and saw a hot air balloon advertising a beer company. He closed his eyes, had a vision, and exclaimed, “I gotta build a balloon that says, ‘Jesus’ on it!” For the next 15 years, Leonard crisscrossed the country in a multi-colored truck covered in Bible verses trying to launch a balloon he sewed together out of bedsheet-sized scrap material that read “GOD IS LOVE,” in giant tattered letters, but never got it off the ground.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p class="p1"&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;Leonard eventually ended up destitute in a remote squatter’s camp in the sweltering California desert where he decided to build a “GOD IS LOVE” mountain to proclaim his testimony. Fellow squatters coined the work, “Salvation Mountain.”&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p class="p1"&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;Humble, stubborn, artistic and outspoken, Leonard spent most of his life in isolation. Despite being orthodox in his theology, his quirky eccentricities were never appreciated by what he called “the big churches.” Reminiscent of a modern day John the Baptist, Leonard was a rock star to seekers from every walk of life and societies misfits. He had to continue on his solo path to fulfill the purpose God had planted in his heart while fending off illegitimate attacks from the county, state, and EPA. But the proud left broken, and the broken left with hope, and by 2009, thousands a week were traveling from all over the world to personally hear “the humble desert hobo” share his “love story.”&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p class="p2"&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;In his final years, already blind, deaf, and slipping into the abyss of dementia, Leonard’s ministry would face it’s greatest opposition yet, which he faced undaunted with his child-like faith. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p class="p2"&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="s1"&gt;&lt;i&gt;The Love Story of Leonard Knight &lt;/i&gt;is an affectionate exploration of his humble beginnings, his years wandering, the moment he received his calling, and his quirky artistic project that was described in 2002 as a “National Treasure” in the US Congressional Record, and is today considered possibly the largest Biblically inspired art-installation on earth.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

          <div class="thumbnail-overlay">
           <a class="hidden-product-link" href="/products/fantastic-failures-true-stories-of-people-who-changed-the-world-by-falling-down-first" itemprop="url">
            Fantastic Failures: True Stories of People Who Changed the World by Falling Down First
           </a>
           <div class="info">
            <!-- product fantastic-failures-true-stories-of-people-who-changed-the-world-by-falling-down-first set-price -->
            <!-- product.price 1299: wh_price 1299-->
            <!-- product.price_min 1299 : wh_price_min 1299 -->
            <!-- product.price_max 2199 : wh_price_max 2199 -->
            <!-- wh_discount_value 1 -->
            <!-- compare_at_price : wh_compare_at_price  -->

            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="books,children-and-young-adult,hardcover-books,new-releases-and-coming-soon-for-summer-fall-2018,paperback-books,positive-parenting-and-child-development,pre-order" data-compare-price="" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description="&lt;p&gt;Available September 11, 2018.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;There is a lot of pressure in today’s society for kids to succeed, but failing is a part of learning how to be a successful person.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;In his teaching career, Luke Reynolds saw the stress and anxiety his students suffered over grades, fitting in, and getting things right the first time. &lt;em&gt;Fantastic Failures&lt;/em&gt; was created for these students to learn that their mistakes and failures do not define their whole lives but help them grow into their potential. Kids will love learning about some of the well-known people who failed before succeeding and will come to understand that failure is a large component of success.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;With stories from people like J. K. Rowling, Albert Einstein, Rosa Parks, Abraham Lincoln, Vincent Van Gogh, Julia Child, Steven Spielberg, and Betsy Johnson, each profile just proves that the greatest mistakes and flops can turn into something amazing. Intermixed throughout the fun profiles, Reynolds spotlights great inventors and scientists who discovered and created some of the most important medicines, devices, and concepts of all time, including lifesaving vaccines and medicines that were stumbled upon by mistake.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;Reynolds's engaging, youthful voice pulls kids into each anecdote much in the same way bestselling &lt;a href=&quot;https://beyondword.com/products/the-rocked-the-world-collection&quot; title=&quot;Rocked the World Collection&quot;&gt;Girls Who Rocked the World and Boys Who Rocked the World&lt;/a&gt; do, making the teaching moments feel more like a friend just retelling a story. Each profile is followed up with advice on how to come back from your own flops and move forward to succeed.&lt;/p&gt;

            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="new-releases-and-coming-soon-for-summer-fall-2018,pre-order" data-compare-price="" data-details-text="View full details" data-full-description='&lt;p&gt;Available September 25, 2018.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Spanda&lt;/b&gt; &lt;i&gt;noun&lt;/i&gt;. 1. Sanskrit meaning "the pulsation before creation" 2. a jolt of inspiration or aha moment that stirs us to action&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;Spanda Cards for the Entrepreneurial Spirit&lt;/i&gt; is the first desktop oracle to combine spiritual wisdom and business know-how. Designed to help you connect to your inner Spanda, these cards move you beyond the habitual knee-jerk reaction and into a still and quiet mindset where creative leaps happen. If you need more clarity, inspiration, direction, and energy, pick up a Spanda card. The aphorism on the card each created using a synthesis of ancient, ageless practices, current thinking in psychology and business, and the authors own insights and experiences is the message you need in this moment to remove the veil from your business or life dilemmas. And the accompanying guidebook offers additional insights and takeaways with short, actionable steps. You may even find the answer to a question you didn t know you needed to ask.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;Like shaking a snow globe, &lt;i&gt;Spanda Cards for the Entrepreneurial Spirit&lt;/i&gt; allows you to tumble around your thoughts and rearrange them into new ways of thinking. Discover how life sparkles with surprise and synchronicity when you tap into your Spanda.&lt;/p&gt;

    <div class="shopify-section page-section" id="shopify-section-1528912390584">
     <div class="homepage_content featured_content clearfix">
      <div class="container">
       <div class="sixteen columns">
        <div class="section clearfix">
         <h2>
          <strong>
           “Sometimes, God picks little people to do things.”
          </strong>
          —Leonard Knight, creator of Salvation Mountain
         </h2>
         <br/>
         <a href="https://beyondword.com/products/the-love-story-of-leonard-knight">
          <img src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/1581/1003/products/Key-Art-Temp_600x@2x.jpg?v=1528841988" style="width: 45%; padding-right: 5%; float: left; border: none;"/>
         </a>
         <p>
          TRUE STORY: In 1971, troubled drifter Leonard Knight had a calling that he was to tell the world that “God is love,” so he created Salvation Mountain in a desolate corner of the California desert. It would remain his home for nearly 30 years, where he would spread that message of God’s love with joy and enthusiasm to anyone who would listen. By 2009, Leonard was receiving thousands of visitors a week from as far away as Mongolia. They were drawn by the unique construction of Salvation Mountain and by Leonard’s unwavering faith.
         </p>
         <p>
          As “the most visited man in America,” Leonard made a profound impact on everyone who came to his mountain. This film is filled with his energy and passion for God’s love and will touch the souls of viewers for years to come.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           “One of the best, most captivating documentaries…
          </em>
          The Love Story of Leonard Knight
          <em>
           is a fascinating movie. …A must-see.”
          </em>
          —Ted Baehr, founder of Movieguide
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>

   </script>
   <script data-no-instant="">
    function inIframe() {
         try {
           return window.self !== window.top;
         } catch (e) {
           return true;
         }
       }
 
       if (!inIframe()){
         InstantClick.on('change', function() {
           if (typeof ga == 'function') {
             ga('send', 'pageview', location.pathname + location.search);
           }
 
           $('head script[src*="shopify"]').each(function() {
             var script = document.createElement('script');
             script.type = 'text/javascript';
             script.src = $(this).attr('src');
 
             $('body').append( script );
           });
 
           var facebookAnalytics = $('head .analytics').text();
           var script = document.createElement( 'script' );
           script.type = 'text/javascript';
           script.text = facebookAnalytics;
           $('body').append( script );
 
           $('html').removeClass('remodal-is-locked');
 
         });
         InstantClick.init();
       }
   </script>
   <script>
   </script>
